SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[Constraints], [p0].[Description], [p0].[Examples], [p0].[Title], [t].[Id], [t].[ExpectedOutput], [t].[Input], [t].[ProblemId], [s].[Id], [s].[Code], [s].[Language], [s].[ProblemId]

    FROM [Problems] AS [p]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [p0]
LEFT JOIN [TestCases] AS [t] ON [p0].[Id] = [t].[ProblemId]

) AS [p0]
